    <script type="text/javascript">

        const progressOverlay = document.querySelector(".progressOverlay");
        const popoverTriggerList = document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="popover"]')
        const popoverList = [...popoverTriggerList].map(popoverTriggerEl => new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTriggerEl))

        // $(document).ready(function() {
        //     console.log("Time until DOMready: ", Date.now()-timerStart);
        // });

        // $(window).on('load', function() {
        //     console.log("Time until everything loaded: ", Date.now()-timerStart);
        // });

        document.addEventListener("readystatechange", (event) => {
            console.log("Time until document.addEventListener [readystatechange]: ( ", document.readyState, " ) ", Date.now()-timerStart);
        });

        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", (event) => {
            console.log("Time until document.addEventListener [DOMContentLoaded]: ", Date.now()-timerStart);
        });

        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
            console.log("Time until window.addEventListener [DOMContentLoaded]: ", Date.now()-timerStart);
        });

        window.addEventListener("load", (event) => {
            console.log("Time until window.addEventListener [load]: ", Date.now()-timerStart);
            progressOverlay.classList.add('loadFinish');
        });


    </script>
